2. Lots of green areas, trees, flowers.
3. Big windows that give lots of light into rooms.
Cons:
1. 2. Reglazed baths - also some paint started to peel off. Guess what, they charged us for reglazing - 350$ per bathtub! Windows look dirty in the gap between two glasses and sometimes there is condensate inside this gap which you cannot wipe.

<Review>We have been living here for the past 8 months so I think now it's time to share a review of these apartments. First of all, this is a very quiet community; Very rarely you would hear loud noises (with the ocasional motorcycle here and there). Management is probably the best we have dealt with in a long time; Upon starting living on the unit we had a problem with our carpet and they promptly replaced it. Maintenance is definitely top notch; Mr Cruz has been nothing but amazing on repairing everything we had issues with, he's very knowledgeable and quick! I mean we came from a `new building` community before and maintenance had to go 2-3 times to repair something or they would take a long time; Here you get a quick response and they fix the issue.

Now for the downsides; I would say I only have 3 things that bother me and those aren't necessarily issues on the community or management but just things that happen:
1) If you have a unit facing Santa Lucia Drive, you will see a bunch of shady people parking there and sometimes teens smoking weed. There's a complex right in front of this one where a lot of smokers come from and they cross the street to smoke on this community side plus some people smoking weed, so you will definitely smell stuff sometimes in the night.
2) There are LOT of bugs, since this community is built around trees and lot of nature you will get your plenty share of mosquitoes, random bugs and of course spiders. I have never seen a crock-roach in my entire time living here which speaks that they keep bad pests under control; But I have definitely dealt with the biggest spiders i've seen in my life haha; I've probably identified 4-5 different species already of spiders.
3) Apartments are a bit dated and well this is a fact since they were built on 1980's but they have been renovated (still you will find some old stuff here and there).

Anyways; Overall my score would have been 4/5 but management and maintenance has been so good that I'm willing to bump it up to 5/5. I truly enjoy living here!</Review><userid>104336615985862798299< /userid><name>Carlos Castro</name></record>

<user>108811498346448355727<//user><user_name>Karl Gendler</user_name><date>1531347493557< /date><Rating>5</Rating><Text>I'll start with the only two downsides to living at Alderwood: the rent and the fitness center. With the new Apple campus opening up nearby, I feel as though I'm paying the premium that comes with demand for local housing for Apple employees. And the fitness center is really small, roughly the size of my single dorm room in college. They stuffed what they could in there, a few treadmills, a bike, an elliptical, a cable machine, and some dumbbells (25lb max), but it's not what I would consider well equipped.

That aside, I really enjoy this place. Here's a list of positive things I've experienced from living at Alderwood:
1. Prometheus management has the right corporate culture. It was intimidating going from knowing my landlord personally to having this large monolithic company to deal with, but in both Prometheus properties I've lived (and in the handful others I've visited/toured), the front desk staff are friendly, helpful, and understanding, going above and beyond to help me with whatever it is I need. Alderwood is no exception to this. They've even jumped my car when the battery died! And Prometheus makes moving between apartments/communities easy (I've already moved twice within their properties).
2. Cruz the maintenance guy has helped me multiple times, and is always clean, polite, responsive, and communicative, and always does quality work.
3. When a flaw in the apartment furnishing damaged some of my belongings, Promethus/Alderwood quickly offered to replace the items at no cost to me, and fixed the apartment furnishing without pulling from my security deposit. Again, company culture done right.
4. The grounds are well kept. Sidewalks are clean, grassy areas are watered and mowed, trees are trimmed, parking lot free of junk, etc.
5. The neighbors are friendly and generally quiet. Alderwood is full of young families so you get the occasional group of children playing outside, bikes and scooters, but overall things are serene. Not at all a college-type scene full of interns.

In all, I very much enjoy living here and would recommend it to anyone so long as the money works (and they don't mind exercising at work or getting a gym membership).</Text><Pictures>None<//Pictures><response>{'time': 1531939936030, 'text': 'Karl, thank you so much for taking time out of your day to share such great feedback. We appreciate the honest comments in areas we can work to improve and have passed along your kudos to the team.  Thank you for sharing.'}< /response>< GmapID>

<Text>This is a SCAM. There were red flags upon the moment we walked in, but we decided to stay in hopes that the meal would make up for it. It did not and we walked out halfway through the omakase. DO NOT BELIEVE THE MICHELIN STAR, it was awarded before the 7-month remodel. I am currently contacting the Michelin Guide to get this star removed and the restaurant re-reviewed.

The service staff were unprofessional, clumsy, and awkward. The kitchen was full of staff just standing there. The place was half empty.

The food was HORRENDOUS. Nothing tasted fresh, everything was bland and tasteless. The first two courses had ingredients that seemed to be sourced from Costco, with horrible quality octopus, shrimp, and vegetables. The sake was served in a wineglass at room temperature.

The first sushi course sealed the deal. The fish was doused in soy sauce, presumably to cover up the lack of flavor and freshness. Whatever flavor did cut through seemed comparable to an all you can eat sushi place. The restaurant tried to pass of fake wasabi as freshly ground wasabi root. The a la carte supplemental menu had outrageous prices for fish that was not sourced from Japan.

I have never left a restaurant halfway through dinner and have never been compelled to write a negative review. Regrettably, the restaurant did not live up to expectations what-so-ever.</Text></record></dataset><record>

Kinjo changed its menu after the renovation this year. They only offer the petite omakase dinner, compared to the full omakase menu before. The taste of the food was not as good as before. Most of the nigiri sushis are seasoned heavily with soy sauce and you cannot taste the flavor of the ingredient itself. The service of the manager (since he was the host at the door, and wear differently compared to our table waiter) was very uncaring and a little bit rude. And yes, I did not tip the full amount.

The noise level in the restaurant was unbearable, unbearable, unbearable. Our ears were raped by the noise from the table behind us for the entire evening. The table behind us was talking and laughing at an unreasonable level. The noise ended up causing me a headache, and I can feel my blood pressure raised.

I will never recommend this restaurant to anyone and I am never coming back again.< /text>

<userid>107828665068533690895</userid>< Review>
I wanted slightly more for the money, but it was good.

The most amazing thing I got was the O-Toro, but it wasn't part of the prix fixe. The way it works is, you make a reservation for the prix fixe meal. Before the desert part, they give you a menu and say, if you want anything additional, please order it now. And so you can get things that you had, or additional things. There's a good chance the main meal won't be enough food for you, and additions aren't cheap. The O-Toro was $28 for one piece of nigiri. Granted, they told me it's the same fish that Jiro gets in Japan, and it was legit. But it's easy to overspend and walk away not really feeling full.<//Review>

< Text>
(Translated by Google) An event conference venue near Chinatown in San Francisco. About 10 minutes by Uber from Union Square. This venue has been around since 1989 and is not too big and convenient. The bus stop is also in front of you. It can accommodate up to 700 people and is fully equipped with WiFi. I visited for the first time as a venue for the pitch contest, and the atmosphere surrounding the stage like an old movie theater was good. It also offers a catering service, and it seemed that it could be used at business meetings. A place you want to use if you have the opportunity.

< review>
A wonderful farm created from the awareness that farm animals deserve to live good lives, with dignity - in the open air, under the sun, eating healthy foods - before being slaughtered. Even as a vegetarian, I'm totally in alignment with this philosophy. < Review>
Good, affordable food, right on the beach. Very cozy vibe. I like the booths. If you‚Äôre looking for an affordable family friendly option with good servers this is an excellent choice. The only reason for 4 stars, rather than 5 is the decor (inside and outside) seems to be from 1982. Throw a fresh coat of paint on this place and it would be awesome. That being said, I love the Blackened Chicken Sandwich (or the Surfin Bird sandwich), it is delicious. They also serve breakfast all day and have daily specials, including an all you can eat spaghetti day. Definitely a worthwhile restaurant choice, not fancy, but friendly, affordable, and tasty.< /Review>

< text>
This place is actually one of my new favorite places for a brunch. Nice location by the beach and those tables by the window facing the beach are heaven. I've been to this place twice since i found it through Yelp.
First experience (May 6) was amazing, my partner and i had marinated tri-tip with 2 eggs, potatoes and bread plus coffee and OJ. Our server was Candis and she was pretty nice and attentive
Second experience (May 21), we ordered exactly the same and it was great as usual but we were really disappointed with the service. Our server was Rachel, she didn't even say hi...grumpy when she took the order, MIA & the worst part was she dropped the check while my partner was still eating without even asking us first if we wanted anything else. We were thinking to order a bottle sparkling wine. My partner was mad because of this so we just paid the bill and moved to Hennessey's Tavern to have some drink.

Updated September 17, 2017:
Today I had brunch here with my partner, we both ordered the same food again and again everytime we eat here. It was 2 over medium eggs with medium rare tri tip, home fries, sourdough toast, coffee and OJ. Our server was Jessy and she was so attentive and friendly. We really had a good time enjoying our brunch facing the beach plus good service from Jessy. Well for that reason Scotty's deserves to get more stars :)

PS: This place provides private parking space for customers.</text>

< Review>
Fantastic and interesting place on the beach, been here a couple of times. Their breakfasts are very very good, especially the Homestyle potatoes and omelettes, the muffins are really good too, last time I was there they had muffins that were made with marmalade inside, which I found to be unusual but tasty. I think the menu said breakfast is available until 3 p.m. The dining areas are set-up up kind of weird since you enter from the center of the building and one side is tables and chairs on the other side is booths I kind of think the at some point there was two separate buildings and somehow they connected them together. The view of the beach from the restaurant is pretty great though, especially in the table and chairs area. There is also apparently a banquet area above the booth side of the building that you can ask about if you need one.</Review>

< Review>
A local's favorite diner type restaurant virtually on the sand. I've patronized this local gem for breakfast/ lunch for years. Nothing fancy. Food is freshly prepared, made to order and the servers are friendly.  A favorite is the breakfast quesadilla... ask for extra Spanish sauce.

The patio portion has skylights and virtually floor to ceiling windows that slide open allowing in the ocean breeze & sounds of the beach & strand. The view is directly, eye-level with the strand & sand allowing diners to watch the passers go by and volleyball players practice on the courts toward the south of the restaurant. (The view is better when the County doesn't have a giant storm-protective sand berm sitting between the restaurant & the ocean. Also, I recall when the section of beach directly out the windows & immediately south of the pier didn't contain the public restrooms & showers and wasn't utilized as an equipment & service vehicle parking area.) The view was nicer when it used to be just sand, volleyball courts, beach goers & the Pacific.</Review>

<Date>1555863968666< /Date><resp>None</resp>< Review>
One of the worst breakfast experiences ever. I got there early as one of the first few people in the restaurant. I waited for my family to get done with Sunrise service on the beach for about 5 mins.  Sitting there waiting for the rest of my party to arrive, no one greeted us or even gave us menus. 15 mins after my party arrived, i finally went to the host stand to get menus and ask who our waitress was. When she was pointed out by another employee, i saw that Mariana, who had passed by me at least 10 times,  decided that she was going to ignore our table and take the orders of five Other groups that came in after us. It took her 20 mins to even acknowledge us...the other waitstaff got us drinks, and 45 mins after that to get some of our food. Mariana kept blaming the Kitchen, but funny to see all the other tables getting their food just fine. After an hour of no food, Mariana kept blaming the kitchen about being backed up and we had to ask the manager twice where our food was. When our food came out, we were missing 4 meals and she had No Clue what we even orders.
"Can't you see how many tables I have, i can't remember everything you ordered", she said.

Wow......just wow. I guess the pen and paper in your hand is just for decorations.

Pouched eggs were solid and the rubbery blueberry pancakes were actually blue...and with 2 small blueberries in each. The last bit of food finally came out 80 mins after we got there.."it's the kitchens fault."

We got a 10% discount for this ridiculously overpriced $100.00 breakfast.

At the end of the day, no one came over to apologize, Mariana never took ownership of anything she did, including not getting our order right. The manager wasn't around or wasn't managing if they were there.

Little bit of business 101... If you can't prepare to handle the rush of a Holiday, and staff your restaurant with the right amount of competent employees....maybe you should find better people to manage your store.< /Review>
